  simple...yet	
  will	
  stay	
  with	
  both	
  you	
  and	
  them	
  for	
  life.
Please	
  do	
  this...	
  it	
  will	
  change	
  your	
  life.
Why	
  am	
  I

  you

  name

  <name>

  I

I	
  trained	
  and	
  became	
  a	
  <CERTIFICATION>	
  Your	
  needs	
  are	
  different.
Your	
  expectations	
  are	
  different.	
  Your	
  wisdom	
  is	
  much	
  deeper.
Which	
  is	
  why	
  I	
  would	
  like	
  to	
  extend	
  to	
  you	
  a	
  free	
  offer.	
  I	
  specialize	
  in	
  <industry>	
  and	
  would	
  love	
  to	
  get	
  a	
  
chance	
  to	
  know	
  you	
  better.	
  No	
  sales	
  pitches	
  or	
  ulterior	
  motives.	
  Just	
  a	
  chance	
  to	
  get	
  together	
  over	
  a	
  coffee	
  or	
  
tea	
  and	
  discuss	
  your	
  life	
  experiences.
If	
  you	
  are	
  interested	
  in	
  talking	
  more	
  about	
  your	
  <finances,	
  insurance	
  needs,	
  etc>,	
  then	
  we	
  certainly	
  can	
  talk	
  
about	
  that	
  as	
  well.	
  But	
  the	
  purpose	
  of	
  this	
  get	
  together	
  is	
  more	
  to	
  talk	
  about	
  you.
Please	
  give	
  me	
  a	
  call	
  at	
  xxx-­‐xxx-­‐xxxx	
  if	
  you	
  are	
  interested.
We	
  can	
  arrange	
  a	
  time	
  that	
  works	
  best	
  for	
  you	
  –	
  and	
  I	
  will	
  also	
  bring	
  with	
  me	
  a

  things	
  you	
  may

  –	
  a	
  free

  card	
  you	
  can	
  use	
  next	
  time	
  you	
  are

  at	
  their	
  <finances,	
  insurance	
  needs,	
  etc>.
There	
  is	
  no	
  catch	
  or	
  ulterior	
  motive.

  call	
  me	
  at	
  xxx-­‐xxx-­‐xxxx	
  and	
  let

  know	
  if	
  you

  and	
  chat.

Article	
  –	
  Senior	
  Citizens	
  Day	
  -­‐	
  August	
  21
Subject	
  lines	
  or	
  headlines	
  for	
  blog	
  post:
st	
  
Do	
  you	
  know	
  what	
  day	
  Sunday,	
  August	
  21 is?
st
Make	
  sure	
  the	
  seniors	
  you	
  know	
  are	
  available	
  Aug	
  21
This	
  Sunday	
  is	
  a	
  very	
  special	
  Seniors	
  Day
Article
Once	
  a	
  year	
  this	
  comes	
  about...	
  and	
  I	
  wanted	
  to	
  make	
  sure	
  you	
  know	
  about	
  it,	
  and	
  hopefully	
  do	
  something	
  
special	
  for	
  it.
st	
  
Sunday,	
  August	
  21 is	
  National	
  Senior	
  Citizens	
  Day.
Maybe	
  you	
  know	
  a	
  few	
  seniors,	
  maybe	
  you	
  are	
  one	
  yourself...
...either	
  way...this	
  is	
  a	
  special	
  day	
  and	
  Seniors	
  deserve	
  special	
  recognition.
Seniors	
  lived	
  through	
  the	
  depression,	
  some	
  fought	
  for	
  our	
  future	
  in	
  World	
  War	
  II.	
  The	
  past	
  50	
  years	
  has	
  sped	
  
up	
  the	
  change	
  they	
  have	
  lived	
  through.
They’ve	
  seen	
  the	
  massive	
  amount	
  of	
  change	
  happening	
  in	
  their	
  world,	
  and	
  within	
  their	
  direct	
  families.
They	
  may	
  not	
  carry	
  cell	
  phones	
  –	
  but	
  are	
  well	
  aware	
  those	
  younger	
  than	
  them	
  do.	
  To	
  seniors,	
  that	
  means	
  
when	
  they	
  phone,	
  someone	
  should	
  answer,	
  or	
  get	
  back	
  to	
  them	
  very	
  shortly.
Seniors	
  changed	
  our	
  world...	
  and	
  continue	
  to	
  do	
  so	
  to	
  this	
  very	
  day.
st
So	
  I	
  would	
  highly	
  recommend	
  you	
  do	
  something	
  special	
  for	
  them	
  on	
  the	
  21 .
One	
  thing	
  they	
  would	
  love	
  from	
  you?	
  Write	
  them	
  an	
  appreciation	
  letter.
	
  
	
  ©	
  Troy	
  White	
  

	
  

Seniors	
  didn’t	
  grow	
  up	
  wired	
  into	
  a	
  computer	
  like	
  todays	
  youth	
  has.	
  They	
  grew	
  up	
  with	
  hand	
  written	
  
everything...	
  and	
  still	
  love	
  it.
Write	
  a	
  senior	
  in	
  your	
  life	
  a	
  letter.	
  Tell	
  them	
  you	
  are	
  thinking	
  about	
  them	
  –	
  and	
  wanted	
  to	
  thank	
  them	
  for	
  
being	
  who	
  they	
  are.
Take	
  them	
  out	
  to	
  lunch	
  and	
  let	
  them	
  read	
  your	
  letter.	
  The	
  impact	
  this	
  little	
  gesture	
  will	
  have	
  is	
  immense.	
  And	
  
if	
  you	
  are	
  a	
  senior	
  –	
  thank	
  you.	
  You	
  have	
  helped	
  raised	
  the	
  future	
  generations.
You	
  helped	
  us	
  maintain	
  our	
  freedom.	
  You	
  laid	
  the	
  foundation	
  for	
  all	
  future	
  generations	
  to	
  piggy	
  back	
  on.	
  
Thank	
  you.	
  I	
  do	
  appreciate	
  you.	
  And	
  would	
  love	
  to	
  say	
  so	
  in	
  person	
  if	
  given	
  the	
  chance.	
  Just	
  say	
  when.	
  <name>

Southpaws	
  Unite...	
  Untraditional	
  Thinkers	
  Are	
  The	
  New	
  Norm
Dear	
  <first	
  name>
th	
  
Sunday,	
  August	
  13 is	
  National	
  Left	
  Handers	
  day...	
  which	
  is	
  why	
  I	
  attached	
  this	
  left	
  handed	
  glove	
  to	
  this	
  letter.
Why	
  would	
  you	
  care	
  one	
  little	
  bit?	
  Fair	
  question...
...Less	
  than	
  12%	
  of	
  the	
  population	
  is	
  left	
  handed.	
  Simple	
  things	
  needed	
  to	
  be	
  reinvented	
  for	
  left	
  handers.	
  
Things	
  that	
  right	
  handers	
  just	
  take	
  for	
  granted...	
  not	
  even	
  having	
  a	
  clue	
  that	
  there	
  was	
  a	
  problem	
  in	
  the	
  first	
  
place.
Which	
  is	
  exactly	
  why	
  I	
  wanted	
  to	
  introduce	
  myself	
  to	
  you.
My	
  name	
  is	
  <name>	
  and	
  I	
  am	
  just	
  like	
  a	
  south	
  paw.	
  I	
  don’t	
  see	
  things	
  like	
  the	
  majority	
  of	
  others	
  do	
  –	
  so	
  I	
  
went	
  out,	
  found	
  a	
  solution,	
  and	
  created	
  a	
  whole	
  new	
  way	
  of	
  doing	
  things.
<BACKGROUND	
  AND	
  CERTIFICATION	
  DETAILS>

  only	
  reason	
  I	
  want	
  you	
  to

  to

  am

  I	
  sought	
  out

to	
  a	
  problem	
  I	
  saw.
And	
  I	
  have	
  one	
  simple	
  request	
  for	
  you.
Can	
  I	
  buy	
  you	
  a	
  coffee	
  or	
  tea?

  like	
  to	
  sit

  30

  chat.	
  No

  No	
  
sales

Just

  a

  for	
  us	
  to	
  get	
  to	
  know	
  each	
  other.

FREE	
  Seminar	
  for	
  <NICHE>	
  Shows	
  You	
  The	
  BEST	
  Way	
  To	
  Stay	
  Healthy...	
  and	
  It	
  Tastes	
  Great	
  Too!
Dear	
  <firstname>
The	
  raw	
  Cacao	
  bean	
  is	
  what	
  makes	
  chocolate.	
  Most	
  people	
  understand	
  that...
...but	
  they	
  may	
  not	
  know	
  that	
  the	
  proper	
  way	
  to	
  pronounce	
  it,	
  is	
  "kuh-­‐KOW"...	
  not	
  “co-­‐	
  co”	
  like	
  most	
  people	
  
think.
...most	
  people	
  also	
  don’t	
  realize	
  that	
  the	
  raw,	
  unprocessed	
  cacao	
  bean	
  is	
  the	
  healthiest	
  food	
  available.	
  On	
  the	
  
ORAC	
  scale	
  (which	
  measures	
  the	
  antioxidant	
  capacities	
  of	
  different	
  foods),	
  cacao	
  beans	
  are	
  at	
  the	
  top	
  of	
  the	
  
charts	
  –	
  more	
  than	
  double	
  that	
  of	
  beans	
  and	
  wild	
  blueberries).
...and...	
  you	
  may	
  not	
  realize	
  that	
  you	
  can	
  attend	
  a	
  very	
  fun	
  chocolate	
  tasting	
  event...	
  free.
Where	
  you	
  can	
  meet	
  new	
  people,	
  sample	
  some	
  of	
  the	
  most	
  delicious	
  chocolates	
  you’ve	
  ever	
  tried...	
  and	
  have	
  
a	
  great	
  time.
My	
  name	
  is	
  <name>	
  and	
  I	
  would	
  like	
  to	
  invite	
  you	
  out	
  to	
  a	
  fun	
  filled	
  afternoon	
  of	
  chocolate	
  tasting,	
  laughter,	
  
and	
  some	
  helpful	
  information	
  for	
  keeping	
  your	
  immune	
  system	
  at	
  it’s	
  strongest.
There	
  is	
  no	
  charge	
  to	
  attend...	
  but	
  there	
  is	
  a	
  catch.
This	
  is	
  only	
  for	
  those	
  50	
  yrs	
  of	
  age	
  and	
  older.	
  You	
  can	
  bring	
  a	
  friend	
  is	
  you	
  like,	
  but	
  we	
  only	
  have	
  room	
  for	
  xx	
  
people	
  like	
  you.

Article	
  –	
  Elephant	
  appreciation	
  day	
  Subject	
  lines	
  or	
  headlines	
  for	
  blog	
  post:	
  Do	
  you	
  know	
  what	
  day	
  Thursday,	
  
September	
  22nd	
  is?	
  Have	
  you	
  ever	
  heard	
  of	
  the	
  book	
  “Modoc”?
This	
  Sunday	
  is	
  a	
  very	
  special	
  Day
	
  
	
  
Article
One	
  of	
  the	
  best	
  true	
  stories	
  ever	
  written	
  is	
  the	
  book	
  Modoc:	
  The	
  True	
  Story	
  of	
  the	
  Greatest	
  Elephant	
  That	
  
Ever	
  Lived	
  by	
  Ralph	
  Helfer.	
  An	
  incredible	
  story	
  talking	
  about	
  the	
  bond	
  a	
  young	
  boy	
  develops	
  with	
  a	
  young	
  
elephant.	
  Unforgettable	
  story	
  is	
  more	
  like	
  it.	
  If	
  you	
  like	
  to	
  pick	
  up	
  a	
  great	
  heart	
  wrenching	
  story,	
  pick	
  this	
  one	
  
up.
	
  

	
  ©	
  Troy	
  White	
  

	
  

They	
  say	
  an	
  elephant	
  never	
  forgets.	
  And	
  I	
  don’t	
  want	
  anyone	
  to	
  forget	
  that	
  September	
  22nd	
  is	
  
Elephant	
  Appreciation	
  Day!
Elephants	
  are	
  a	
  symbol	
  of	
  wisdom	
  in	
  Asian	
  cultures	
  and	
  are	
  famed	
  for	
  their	
  memory	
  and	
  intelligence,
They	
  also	
  show	
  us	
  what	
  can	
  happen	
  when	
  old	
  ideas	
  and	
  beliefs	
  remain	
  unchallenged.
When	
  elephants	
  are	
  young	
  and	
  in	
  captivity,	
  they	
  are	
  chained	
  with	
  thick	
  ropes	
  to	
  ensure	
  they	
  don’t	
  escape.	
  As	
  
they	
  get	
  older,	
  those	
  shackles	
  are	
  kept	
  the	
  same	
  size...	
  and	
  the	
  elephant	
  never	
  thinks	
  to	
  challenge	
  the	
  strength	
  
of	
  the	
  shackles.	
  All	
  they	
  have	
  to	
  do	
  is	
  challenge	
  it	
  once	
  and	
  it	
  would	
  quickly	
  dissolve	
  under	
  the	
  immense	
  power	
  
of	
  these	
  giants.
Which	
  is	
  just	
  like	
  the	
  way	
  much	
  of	
  the	
  business	
  world	
  is...	
  unchallenged.
I	
  don’t	
  see	
  things	
  like	
  the	
  majority	
  of	
  others	
  do	
  –	
  so	
  I	
  went	
  out,	
  found	
  a	
  solution,	
  and	
  created	
  a	
  whole	
  new	
  
way	
  of	
  doing	
  things.
<SOME	
  BRIEF	
  BACKGROUND	
  ON	
  WHERE	
  YOU	
  CAME	
  FROM	
  AND	
  WHAT	
  MAKES	
  YOU	
  DIFFERENT>	
  I	
  broke	
  the	
  
traditional	
  mold	
  used	
  in	
  my	
  industry	
  ...	
  and	
  I	
  love	
  it...	
  so	
  do	
  my	
  clients.	
  And	
  I	
  challenge	
  you	
  to	
  demand	
  more	
  
and	
  press	
  yourself	
  to	
  push	
  the	
  boundaries.	
  Then	
  let	
  me	
  know	
  what	
  you	
  find.
<name>

FREE	
  Beer	
  Tasting	
  and	
  Pairing	
  Seminar	
  ...for	
  <NICHE>	
  Only
Did	
  you	
  know	
  that	
  there	
  have	
  been	
  different	
  styles	
  of	
  beer	
  made	
  since	
  2,000	
  BC?	
  That’s	
  a	
  lot	
  of	
  brewing	
  
experience.
In	
  4,100	
  years,	
  they	
  must	
  have	
  learned	
  a	
  thing	
  or	
  two	
  about	
  beer	
  quality,	
  tasting,	
  and	
  even	
  pairing	
  the	
  right	
  
beer	
  with	
  different	
  foods.
So	
  why	
  is	
  that	
  most	
  of	
  us	
  who	
  enjoy	
  a	
  cold	
  one	
  every	
  once	
  in	
  a	
  while	
  typically	
  stick	
  what	
  the	
  brands	
  and	
  styles	
  
of	
  beer	
  that	
  we	
  know?
With	
  the	
  hundreds,	
  even	
  thousands,	
  of	
  different	
  alternatives	
  to	
  the	
  same-­‐old,	
  same-­‐old	
  beer	
  we	
  always	
  
drink...	
  why	
  don’t	
  we	
  try	
  new	
  kinds?
Mainly	
  it	
  comes	
  down	
  to	
  knowledge.
Not	
  know	
  what	
  types	
  of	
  beers	
  we	
  would	
  like.	
  And	
  not	
  know	
  what	
  types	
  of	
  beers	
  that	
  are	
  available	
  (even	
  
knowing	
  all	
  the	
  different	
  kinds,	
  brands	
  and	
  styles	
  can	
  seem	
  overwhelming).
My	
  name	
  is	
  <name>	
  and	
  I	
  would	
  like	
  to	
  invite	
  you	
  out	
  to	
  a	
  fun	
  filled	
  afternoon	
  of	
  beer	
  tasting,	
  laughter,	
  and	
  
some	
  helpful	
  information

Not	
  everyone	
  loves	
  beer.
But	
  beer	
  certainly	
  deserves	
  a	
  bit	
  of	
  respect	
  from	
  everyone.
Did	
  you	
  know	
  that	
  there	
  have	
  been	
  different	
  styles	
  of	
  beer	
  made	
  since	
  2,000	
  BC?
That’s	
  a	
  lot	
  of	
  brewing	
  experience.
In	
  4,100	
  years,	
  they	
  must	
  have	
  learned	
  a	
  thing	
  or	
  two	
  about	
  beer	
  quality,	
  tasting,	
  and	
  even	
  pairing	
  the	
  right	
  
beer	
  with	
  different	
  foods.
So	
  why	
  is	
  that	
  most	
  of	
  us	
  who	
  enjoy	
  a	
  cold	
  one	
  every	
  once	
  in	
  a	
  while	
  typically	
  stick	
  what	
  the	
  brands	
  and	
  styles	
  
of	
  beer	
  that	
  we	
  know?
With	
  the	
  hundreds,	
  even	
  thousands,	
  of	
  different	
  alternatives	
  to	
  the	
  same-­‐old	
  same-­‐old	
  beer	
  we	
  always	
  drink...	
  
why	
  don’t	
  we	
  try	
  new	
  kinds?
Mainly	
  it	
  comes	
  down	
  to	
  knowledge.
Not	
  know	
  what	
  types	
  of	
  beers	
  we	
  would	
  like.	
  And	
  not	
  know	
  what	
  types	
  of	
  beers	
  that	
  are	
  available	
  (even	
  
knowing	
  all	
  the	
  different	
  kinds,	
  brands	
  and	
  styles	
  can	
  seem	
  overwhelming).
My	
  name	
  is	
  <name>	
  and	
  I	
  would	
  like	
  to	
  invite	
  you	
  out	
  to	
  a	
  fun	
  filled	
  afternoon	
  of	
  beer	
  tasting,	
  laughter,	
  and	
  
some	
  helpful	
  information	
  for	
  matching	
  beers	
  with	
  foods.	
  We	
  may	
  even	
  talk	
  about	
  some	
  of	
  the	
  recent	
  research	
  
out	
  that	
  shows	
  the	
  immense	
  health	
  benefits	
  in	
  certain	
  tupes	
  of	
  beer.
There	
  is	
  no	
  charge	
  to	
  attend...	
  but	
  there	
  is	
  a	
  catch.
This	
  is	
  only	
  for	
  those	
  <NICHE>.	
  You	
  can	
  bring	
  a

  we	
  only	
  have	
  room	
  for	
  xx

  like

Article	
  –	
  National	
  Bosses	
  Day	
  	
  
Subject	
  lines	
  or	
  headlines	
  for	
  blog	
  post:	
  Ever	
  wanted	
  to	
  blow	
  up	
  your	
  boss?	
  Your	
  boss	
  wants	
  you	
  to	
  read	
  
this	
  Your	
  old	
  boss	
  wants	
  you	
  to	
  read	
  this	
  Article	
  There	
  are	
  3	
  kinds	
  of	
  bosses	
  in	
  this	
  world:
• Those	
  we	
  just	
  can’t	
  seem	
  to	
  get	
  along	
  with...	
  no	
  matter	
  how	
  hard	
  we	
  try.	
  They	
  are	
  the	
  beurocrats	
  that	
  value	
  
pushing	
  paper	
  over	
  actual	
  productive	
  work.	
  They	
  are	
  the	
  nasty	
  Nancies	
  that	
  take	
  great	
  pleasure	
  in	
  
	
  
	
  ©	
  Troy	
  White	
  
	
  

demeaning	
  you.	
  They	
  are	
  the	
  jerks	
  that	
  think	
  their	
  job	
  as	
  a	
  boss	
  is	
  to	
  make	
  sure	
  you	
  are	
  always	
  worried	
  
about	
  being	
  fired.	
  
• There	
  are	
  those	
  that	
  are	
  a	
  dream	
  to	
  work	
  with.	
  They	
  are	
  encouraging.	
  They	
  are	
  trusting.	
  They	
  value	
  your	
  
hard	
  work	
  and	
  stand	
  behind	
  you	
  anytime	
  something	
  goes	
  a	
  little	
  haywire.	
   Then	
  there	
  are	
  the	
  types	
  of	
  
bosses	
  that	
  few	
  people	
  think	
  about...	
  our	
  customers.	
  Whenever	
  you	
  buy	
  something	
  from	
  a	
  company,	
  
you	
  are	
  their	
  boss.	
  You	
  can	
  complain,	
  you	
  can	
  encourage,	
  or	
  you	
  can	
  take	
  your	
  money	
  elsewhere,	
  and	
  
encourage	
  everyone	
  else	
  to	
  do	
  the	
  same.	
  
"There	
  is	
  only	
  one	
  boss.	
  The	
  customer.	
  And	
  he	
  can	
  fire	
  everybody	
  in	
  the	
  company	
  from	
  the	
  chairman	
  on	
  down,	
  
simply	
  by	
  spending	
  his	
  money	
  somewhere	
  else."-­‐	
  Sam	
  Walton.
It	
  has	
  never	
  been	
  easier	
  than	
  now	
  to	
  get	
  your	
  negative	
  experiences	
  publicized.	
  The	
  internet.	
  All	
  these	
  things	
  
like	
  Facebook.	
  Email.	
  Blogs.	
  All	
  of	
  them	
  are	
  perfect	
  for	
  spreading	
  the	
  word.	
  Good	
  and	
  bad.
In	
  my	
  business,	
  my	
  customers	
  and	
  clients	
  are	
  kings	
  and	
  queens.	
  They	
  are	
  the	
  ones	
  in	
  control...	
  and	
  if	
  I	
  don’t	
  do	
  
my	
  job	
  right,	
  they	
  ensure	
  I	
  don’t	
  make	
  money	
  and	
  cannot	
  feed	
  my	
  family.
I	
  personally	
  work	
  very	
  hard	
  to	
  ensure	
  my	
  clients	
  DO	
  get	
  the	
  best	
  experience	
  possible.
In	
  fact,	
  I	
  love	
  working	
  with	
  <NICHE>.	
  I	
  also	
  knew	
  that	
  most	
  of	
  them	
  were	
  fed	
  up	
  with	
  the	
  present	
  state	
  of	
  
customer	
  service	
  out	
  there.	
  So	
  I	
  went	
  out	
  and	
  found	
  the	
  training	
  that	
  solves	
  this	
  problem
As	
  a	
  <TITLE>,	
  I	
  now	
  understand	
  what	
  <NICHE>	
  want,	
  and	
  guarantee	
  to	
  deliver	
  the	
  experience	
  they	
  desire.
I	
  also	
  encourage	
  you	
  to	
  do	
  the	
  same.	
  If	
  you	
  have	
  customers,	
  invest	
  in	
  more	
  training	
  to	
  find	
  out	
  what	
  they	
  
want.	
  If	
  you	
  don’t	
  have	
  customers,	
  you	
  still	
  have	
  others	
  in	
  your	
  life	
  you	
  interact	
  with.	
  Ask	
  them	
  more	
  
questions...	
  more	
  personal	
  questions.	
  Find	
  out	
  who	
  they	
  really	
  are.	
  Find	
  out	
  their	
  dreams,	
  their	
  goals,	
  their	
  
passions.	
  Talk	
  about	
  their	
  interests...	
  and	
  they	
  will	
  soon	
  become	
  even	
  closer	
  clients	
  and	
  friends.	
  Certainly	
  
makes	
  for	
  some	
  great	
  connections	
  and	
  friendships!

Dear	
  <first	
  name>	
  Who	
  knew?	
  It’s	
  not	
  Halloween	
  or	
  Valentines	
  day	
  –	
  it’s	
  October	
  17 and	
  is	
  official	
  the	
  
sweetest	
  day	
  that	
  the	
  candy	
  industry	
  sells	
  75%	
  of	
  their	
  business.
Herbert	
  Birch	
  Kingston,	
  a	
  philanthropist	
  and	
  candy	
  company	
  employee	
  wanted	
  to	
  bring	
  happiness	
  into	
  the	
  
lives	
  of	
  orphans	
  and	
  others	
  who	
  were	
  forgotten.
	
  
	
  ©	
  Troy	
  White	
  

	
  

With	
  the	
  help	
  of	
  friends,	
  he	
  began	
  to	
  distribute	
  candy	
  and	
  small	
  gifts	
  to	
  the	
  underprivileged.
The	
  tradition	
  caught	
  on	
  with	
  movie	
  star	
  Ann	
  Pennington	
  presenting	
  2,200	
  Cleveland	
  newspaper	
  boys	
  with	
  
boxes	
  of	
  candy	
  to	
  express	
  gratitude	
  for	
  their	
  service	
  to	
  the	
  public.
Another	
  popular	
  movie	
  star,	
  Theda	
  Bara,	
  distributed	
  10,000	
  boxes	
  of	
  candy	
  to	
  people	
  in	
  Cleveland	
  hospitals	
  
and	
  also	
  gave	
  candy	
  to	
  all	
  who	
  came	
  to	
  watch	
  her	
  film	
  in	
  a	
  local	
  theater.
Often	
  we	
  take	
  things	
  for	
  granted...	
  like	
  the	
  assumption	
  that	
  Halloween	
  or	
  Valentines	
  day	
  would	
  be	
  the	
  
greatest	
  sales	
  day	
  for	
  sweets.
What	
  does	
  this	
  have	
  to	
  do	
  with	
  you?
I	
  wanted	
  to	
  show	
  a	
  little	
  appreciation	
  for	
  the	
  simple	
  things	
  in	
  life	
  and	
  the	
  little	
  surprises	
  is	
  one	
  of	
  the	
  trends	
  
that	
  fuels	
  this	
  celebration.
Please	
  accept	
  this	
  sweet	
  gift	
  on	
  my	
  behalf...	
  and	
  I	
  would	
  love	
  to	
  offer	
  you	
  a	
  coffee	
  or	
  tea	
  (cookies	
  on	
  me!).

  name	
  is	
  <name>	
  and	
  I	
  wanted	
  to	
  introduce	
  myself	
  to	
  you	
  in	
  an	
  unusual	
  way...

  probably	
  are

  materials.	
  Always

you

Dear	
  <firstname>
You	
  know	
  all	
  the	
  stats	
  about	
  Boomers	
  and	
  Seniors.
You	
  are	
  one,	
  so	
  you	
  will	
  fully	
  appreciate	
  what	
  I	
  am	
  about	
  to	
  share.
A	
  couple	
  of	
  the	
  best	
  parts	
  about	
  being	
  over	
  50	
  right	
  now?
...the	
  medical	
  breakthroughs	
  happening	
  every	
  day	
  of	
  the	
  year	
  that	
  give	
  greater	
  health	
  and	
  longevity
...the	
  fact	
  that	
  there	
  are	
  so	
  many	
  others	
  around

  a	
  similar	
  age,	
  and	
  are	
  looking

  fun

do

  one

  Are	
  we	
  ready	
  for	
  it?

  name	
  is	
  <name>

  I	
  would

  recent

  medical

  50.

EMAIL NEWSLETTER
Subject: Criminal acts at Christmas... making sure you aren’t part
Hi <firstname>, Are you breaking the law?
Not exactly something that we plan to do. But something that far too many people do at this time of year.
st
In honor of the Anniversary of the 1 Taxicab in use in London (1897), I want to talk to you about a very
important issue that may impact you and/or your family.
Taxi cabs are a part of everyday life.
Some people use them for all their transportation, others use them infrequently for times they want to go out and
have a little ‘cheer’.
We are in the midst of the busiest shopping season of the year... as well as the busiest party season of the year.
Alcohol is freely enjoyed and used during the Holiday season.
You may even be having a get together at home, or taking others out for dinner and drinks (both of which are
good ideas, but care must be taken).
The opportunities are everywhere... company parties, supplier parties, family get togethers, friends gathering...
each of them a fun time.
For the coming month, I wanted to extend some ideas to make your holiday season a little safer for you and
your family.
	
  

	
  ©	
  Troy	
  White	
  

	
  

First, the facts: * Impaired driving is the leading criminal cause of death in all of Canada
* In 2007, it was estimated that 3,045 individuals were killed in motor vehicle crashes in Canada. MADD
Canada estimates that at a minimum 1,239 of these fatalities were impairment-related. * The rules apply to the
water as well! In 2005, it was reported that there were 126 boating fatalities, 47 of which involved known or
suspected alcohol use (37%!!)
Some tips to make your month safe:
. 1) Know the limits! Some provinces are now at .05 blood alcohol level. Depending on the size of person, that
can be one single drink that makes it a criminal act to drive.
. 2) Report bad or impaired drivers you see on the road. If you don’t, how can you be sure it isn’t someone you
know that they run into a couple miles down the road? A friend? Family member? Call the police
immediately if you see any signs of impaired driving.
. 3) Be a responsible host. If you are having others over for some Christmas cheer, make sure you are
prepared. First, have lots of hearty food available for people to snack on. Breads and dips or sandwiches
are perfect for parties. Watch what is happening. You are the host and part of your job as a host is to pay
attention to how much people are drinking. If they are driving, make sure you let them know that you
have taxis or driving services available. Even offer to make it easier for them to get their car the next
day. If you are entertaining people that are drinking, it IS your responsibility to ensure all of your guests
stay off the roads while impaired.
. 4) Be a good person and don’t let your friends and family drive after drinking. Let them borrow a couch, or a
spare bed... just don’t let them drive.
. 5) Tell your kids NOT to get in the car with someone who has been drinking – you’ll pick them up and they
won’t get in trouble for calling you! As well, you should also never get in a car with a driver that has
been drinking.
. 6) If you are entertaining – make sure you have all kinds of different non-alcoholic drinks as well. Coffee,
pops. juice and water.
These may be common sense tips for the holiday season, but they are ideas you need to follow.
If you are having a fun event, make sure you have ample food, taxi numbers or coupons on hand, and sufficient
quantities of non-alcoholic beverages available.
The point is not to put a damper on some holiday fun, but to ensure you are safe while doing so. So enjoy... just
not too much. Taxi Cabs are the cheapest thing going... ...especially when you consider the alternatives!
<signature>
PS: I am hosting a very intimate group for a private champagne and wine tasting at <JV partner companies
name>. We will be adhered, of course, to all of the rules and suggestions above. If you are interested in
attending, please contact me as soon as possible as we only have room for xx people. What a great way to get
out – have some fun – and meeting some great people. Please join us - call me direct at xxx.xxx.xxxx and we
can hold you a spot or two.

HUMAN RIGHTS DIRECT MAIL PIECE
	
  

	
  ©	
  Troy	
  White	
  

	
  

Possible envelope ideas: Your Own Personal/Business Bill of rights printed out,
Dear friend, As you can see, I have attached something quite unusual with this letter. Why? Two reason
actually:
First, December 10th is Human Rights Day. We all have rights. Sometimes others try and take those away
without our permission. So I have included a little something to show you that I am thinking of you.
Second, I wanted to make sure that you understand who I am and why I have developed my own Bill of Rights.
The formal establishment of the December 10

th

Human Rights Day occurred in December, 1950.

For 60 years now, we have given people an opportunity to celebrate the fact that we do need to acknowledge
our rights and understand what they mean. In 2009, the focus was on non-discrimination. “All human beings
are born free and equal in dignity and rights”.
These first few famous words of the Universal Declaration of Human Rights established 60 years ago the basic
premise of international human rights law. Yet today, the fight against discrimination remains a daily struggle
for millions around the globe.
Please have a look through my own Bill of Rights, written for you. And, as you enjoy the holiday season
festivities, please take some time to reflect on the gift of living in a world, a nation, a country, society,
community, and family where the rights of each individual are embraced, celebrated and protected. Have a safe
and enjoyable holiday season. I am thinking of you and want to wish you all the best in the coming year.
<signature>
PS: I am hosting a very intimate group for a private champagne and wine tasting ay <JV partner companies
name>. If you are interested in attending, please contact me as soon as possible as we only have room for xx
people. What a great way to get out – have some fun – and meeting some great people. Please join us - call me
direct at xxx.xxx.xxxx and we can hold you a spot or two.

December Customer Event – Champagne and Wine Tasting

December: Champagne & Wine Tasting for Non-connoisseurs
What better way to acknowledge your clients than with a celebration party. Everyone loves a great party –
especially when you combine it with an educational event.
Partnering up with a local Wine Merchant is a fantastic way to build your exposure and create strong bonds
with your clients.
The champagne and wine tasting idea is quite simple, we suggest that you find a Joint Venture Partner who is in
the wine business, has a facility that can be used for group demonstrations, and someone who is has the skills to
teach to a group. Ideally, your potential JV partner also has their own portfolio of mature clients that he/she can
promote this event to. While that is not the point, it most definitely is an added bonus.
	
  

	
  ©	
  Troy	
  White	
  

	
  

You will benefit from exposure to your JV’s clients; he/she will benefit from exposure to yours; and you both
will benefit from exposure to the new prospects that attend this event.
In the first week of November we suggest that you begin your search for the perfect JV partner for this event.
They could be a small wine dealer with a side or back room set aside for tasting. The key consideration is that
you find a venue where you can hold this class that can actually give them room to provide different samples,
and have a place where everyone there can properly hear the wine expert talking about the different kinds of
wines.
Once you have the venue established and you’ve arranged your JV, you and your JV partner should begin
promoting this seminar in the last week of November. Keep this a small group of 10 or 15 at most. It is only
natural that a wine tasting should be a little more intimate than a larger client event./ That also makes it easier to
fill, and builds some exclusivity into your event.
Two weeks before the seminar, send an email blast or a direct mail campaign to the people on your database,
and ask your JV partner to do the same. Don’t hesitate to send this to both men and women, as the women will
encourage their husbands to attend.
The week before the seminar, encourage the local media to run advertisements to inform their readers of this
seminar. When you are running the ad in the paper, your newspaper can provide stock photography that suits
the ad. You will also want your JV Partner to post signs in their place of business to promote this event. The
signs can be enlargements of the newspaper template we’ve provided.
On the day of the event, be sure to have a sign-up form for attendees.
Make sure you capture the names, addresses and email addresses of everyone who attends so you can use this
information in other marketing efforts. Note: at the bottom of the form have a statement that indicates that you
are collecting this information to use to inform the participants about further ideas involving food and wine, as
well as receiving future promotions from you and your JV partner’s companies.
After the seminar, take the time to send a thank you to your clients who brought friends and neighbors to the
event. Make sure that you let them know you appreciate them for doing this for you. When you express that
gratitude, they will know it is coming from your heart, and they will go out of their way to do more for you in
the future.
And finally, make sure that you set up a communication flow with the new people who came to this seminar.

that?

Dear	
  <name>

  happens	
  when	
  you	
  pull	
  this	
  frog	
  back	
  6	
  inches?

  takes	
  a	
  giant	
  leap	
  forward.

  if	
  you	
  pull	
  it	
  too	
  far	
  back,	
  it	
  snaps	
  and	
  is	
  useless.

  Dear	
  <<first	
  name>>,
Here’s	
  how	
  you	
  can	
  add	
  an	
  extra	
  $xxxx	
  in	
  profit	
  to	
  your	
  bottom	
  line	
  without	
  lifting	
  a	
  finger	
  or	
  investing	
  a	
  cent.
I	
  have	
  a	
  profitable	
  proposition	
  for	
  you	
  –	
  one	
  that	
  could	
  be	
  repeated	
  time	
  and	
  time	
  again.	
  My	
  name	
  is	
  _____	
  
and	
  I’m	
  a	
  director	
  of	
  _____.	
  I	
  specialize	
  in	
  ______.
I	
  am	
  presently	
  setting	
  up	
  joint-­‐venture	
  projects	
  that	
  let	
  you	
  gain	
  the	
  maximum	
  profits	
  possible	
  from	
  your	
  
customer	
  list.
Especially	
  since	
  most	
  of	
  your	
  customers	
  are	
  small	
  to	
  medium	
  size	
  business	
  owners	
  –	
  the	
  ideal	
  customer	
  profile	
  
for	
  this	
  type	
  of	
  project.	
  Remember,	
  this	
  is	
  extra	
  income	
  above	
  and	
  beyond	
  what	
  you	
  are	
  already	
  making	
  each	
  
month.
Here’s	
  how	
  it	
  works....
I	
  have	
  tested	
  specific	
  letters	
  directed	
  at	
  business	
  owners.	
  Mailing	
  to	
  our	
  own	
  list	
  of	
  customers	
  has	
  generated	
  a	
  
response	
  of	
  up	
  to	
  x%.	
  What	
  I	
  am	
  proposing,	
  is	
  testing	
  these	
  proven	
  offers	
  to	
  your	
  list	
  of	
  customers.	
  If	
  they	
  are	
  
as	
  profitable	
  as	
  I	
  expect,	
  you’ll	
  be	
  making	
  extra	
  profits	
  and
your	
  customers	
  will	
  be	
  getting	
  profit	
  enhancing	
  information	
  worth	
  many	
  times	
  what	
  they	
  pay	
  for	
  it.
Here’s	
  how	
  our	
  joint	
  venture	
  would	
  work,	
  and	
  the	
  benefits	
  you’ll	
  get...
I’ll	
  supply	
  you	
  with	
  a	
  sample	
  endorsement	
  letter	
  to	
  put	
  on	
  your	
  letterhead	
  and	
  stationery.	
  This	
  is	
  the	
  letter	
  
that	
  will	
  introduce	
  our	
  products	
  and	
  my	
  company	
  to	
  your	
  subscribers.
In	
  exchange	
  for	
  your	
  endorsement,	
  you’ll	
  receive	
  xx%	
  of	
  the	
  profits.	
  I’ll	
  pay	
  for	
  all	
  the	
  costs	
  of	
  production,	
  
mailing,	
  postage	
  and	
  fulfillment	
  of	
  the	
  orders.	
  This	
  means	
  you	
  have	
  no-­‐risk	
  whatever	
  in	
  this	
  project.

  Troy

Endorsed	
  offers	
  like	
  the	
  one	
  I	
  am	
  proposing	
  usually	
  produce	
  similar	
  results.
All	
  orders	
  can	
  be	
  taken	
  by	
  you	
  for	
  total	
  accountability	
  or	
  I	
  can	
  take	
  them	
  through	
  my	
  office	
  and	
  give	
  you	
  full	
  
auditing	
  rights.	
  We	
  track	
  the	
  source	
  of	
  every	
  order	
  we	
  get	
  in	
  our	
  office.	
  We	
  will	
  pay	
  you	
  your	
  share	
  at	
  the	
  end	
  
of	
  each	
  month.	
  It’s	
  in	
  our	
  interest	
  to	
  do	
  this,	
  since	
  once	
  you	
  see	
  how	
  lucrative	
  this	
  is,	
  you’ll	
  want	
  to	
  do	
  other	
  
joint	
  ventures	
  with	
  us.
That’s	
  an	
  overview	
  of	
  how	
  it	
  would	
  work.	
  Basically,	
  I’ll	
  pay	
  all	
  the	
  costs,	
  do	
  all	
  the	
  work,	
  and	
  make	
  sure	
  the	
  
project	
  happens	
  as	
  it’s	
  supposed	
  to.	
  All	
  you	
  have	
  to	
  do	
  is	
  approve	
  the	
  copy,	
  and	
  send	
  me	
  a	
  sampling	
  of	
  your	
  
list	
  of	
  customers	
  together	
  with	
  your	
  letterheads.
I	
  would	
  like	
  to	
  test	
  600	
  names	
  mailed	
  first	
  class.	
  This	
  will	
  allow	
  us	
  to	
  see	
  quickly	
  what	
  sort	
  of	
  results	
  we	
  can	
  
expect	
  from	
  the	
  rest	
  of	
  your	
  list.	
  Once	
  we’ve	
  verified	
  the	
  results	
  we	
  can	
  proceed	
  with	
  mailing	
  the	
  rest	
  of	
  your	
  
list	
  and	
  banking	
  the	
  money.
To	
  get	
  the	
  ball	
  rolling	
  on	
  this,	
  please	
  call	
  me	
  on	
  xxx.xxx.xxxx	
  I	
  hope	
  you	
  are	
  as	
  keen	
  to	
  test	
  this	
  project	
  as	
  I	
  am.	
  
I	
  think	
  it’s	
  a	
  winner	
  for

Headline	
  Formulas	
  To	
  Use	
  	
  
(email	
  subject	
  lines	
  –	
  facebook	
  updates	
  –	
  twitter	
  updates)	
  
	
  ==	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  <<<<<	
  ===	
  >>>>>	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =	
  =
Headlines	
  are	
  what	
  makes	
  your	
  marketing	
  work...	
  or	
  bomb.	
  It	
  really	
  is	
  that	
  straightforward.	
  IF	
  you	
  have	
  a	
  bad	
  
headline,	
  your	
  ad	
  won’t	
  work	
  or	
  your	
  site	
  won’t	
  keep	
  visitors.	
  If	
  you	
  have	
  no	
  headline,	
  welcome	
  to	
  the	
  club!	
  
Few	
  companies	
  or	
  professionals	
  have	
  or	
  use	
  headlines.	
  To	
  most,	
  the	
  company	
  name	
  is	
  a	
  headline.	
  Wrong.
Your	
  customers	
  don’t	
  really	
  care	
  what	
  your	
  company	
  name	
  is.
They	
  care	
  about	
  what	
  you	
  can	
  do	
  to	
  help	
  them.	
  And	
  your	
  company	
  name	
  doesn’t	
  help	
  them	
  at	
  all.
Nor	
  does	
  cutesy	
  sayings.	
  Here	
  is	
  a	
  list	
  of	
  some	
  of	
  the	
  best	
  headlines	
  ever	
  written.	
  These	
  headlines	
  got	
  people	
  
to	
  read.	
  They	
  made	
  the	
  owners	
  a	
  bundle.	
  And	
  they	
  are	
  easily	
  modified	
  to	
  suite	
  your	
  business.	
  Think	
  of	
  each	
  of	
  
these	
  like	
  a	
  template.
For	
  example:
The	
  headline	
  here	
  made	
  millions	
  for	
  its	
  owner:	
  They	
  Laughed	
  When	
  I	
  Sat	
  Down	
  At	
  The	
  Piano	
  -­‐	
  But	
  When	
  I	
  
Started	
  to	
  Play!
Which	
  could	
  be	
  modified	
  to:
They	
  Snickered	
  When	
  I	
  Left	
  My	
  Corporate	
  Job	
  To	
  Be	
  an	
  Advisor	
  -­‐	
  But	
  When	
  I	
  Became	
  Wealthy	
  With	
  My	
  Own	
  
Advice!
	
  

	
  ©	
  Troy	
  White	
  

	
  

They	
  Laughed	
  When	
  I	
  Wrote	
  My	
  First	
  Book	
  -­‐	
  But	
  When	
  It	
  Hit	
  The	
  Best	
  Seller	
  Shelves!
So	
  here	
  is	
  the	
  template	
  for	
  you	
  to	
  play	
  with...
They	
  Laughed	
  When	
  I	
  ____________	
  -­‐	
  But	
  When	
  I	
  _______________!	
  Simple	
  –	
  right?	
  These	
  formulas	
  work,	
  
but	
  you	
  have	
  to	
  try	
  a	
  bunch	
  of	
  variations.
Headline	
  writers	
  will	
  often	
  create	
  20,	
  30	
  –	
  even	
  50	
  variations	
  of	
  a	
  headline	
  before	
  hitting	
  on	
  the	
  one	
  that	
  wins.
Your	
  best	
  bet?
Go	
  through	
  these	
  2	
  lists	
  and	
  write	
  out	
  at	
  least	
  20	
  or	
  30	
  variations.
You	
  can	
  use	
  them	
  as	
  headlines	
  –	
  as	
  Facebook	
  updates	
  -­‐	
  as	
  Tweets	
  –	
  as	
  email	
  subject	
  lines.
They	
  are	
  powerful	
  and	
  you	
  want	
  to	
  keep	
  them	
  in	
  a	
  secure	
  place.
Remember:	
  One	
  good	
  headline	
  can	
  keep	
  leads	
  and	
  new	
  business	
  flowing	
  to	
  you	
  for	
  many	
  years	
  to	
  come.	
  So	
  it	
  
is	
  a	
  good	
  idea	
  to	
  invest	
  a	
  few	
  hours	
  with	
  pen	
  and	
  paper	
  writing	
  headlines.
Off	
  we	
  go...

  Cosmopolitan	
  Headlines.
Don’t	
  laugh.

  write

  paid

  do	
  so.
Why?

  one	
  GREAT	
  headline	
  can	
  sell

  of	
  their	
  magazine.

If	
  I	
  can	
  leave	
  one	
  thing	
  with	
  you	
  in	
  our	
  work	
  together,	
  it’s	
  this...
AGGRESSIVE	
  MARKETING	
  IMPROVES	
  CASH	
  FLOW.
Being	
  timid	
  or	
  easily	
  offended	
  by	
  snide	
  comments	
  by	
  friends,	
  family,	
  or	
  industry	
  counterparts	
  will	
  get	
  you	
  NO	
  
WHERE.
But	
  learning	
  more	
  about	
  being	
  and	
  thinking	
  like	
  a	
  marketer	
  WILL	
  GET	
  YOU	
  ANYTHING	
  YOU	
  WANT.
It’s	
  all	
  about	
  getting	
  stuff	
  done	
  and	
  in	
  front	
  of	
  your	
  clients	
  and	
  prospective	
  clients	
  consistently.
Multiple	
  medias	
  combined	
  works	
  best.
You	
  will	
  get	
  everyone	
  under	
  the	
  sun	
  instantly	
  becoming	
  a	
  marketing	
  expert	
  when	
  you	
  show	
  them	
  these	
  
letters,	
  emails,	
  or	
  pieces	
  in	
  this	
  kit.
Yet	
  I	
  would	
  be	
  willing	
  to	
  bet	
  they	
  have	
  NEVER	
  ran	
  a	
  successful	
  marketing	
  campaign	
  in	
  their	
  life...	
  consistently.
I	
  have.
And	
  this	
  ‘hokey’	
  approach	
  works	
  in	
  every	
  market	
  you	
  could	
  possibly	
  imagine.
I’ll	
  prove	
  it	
  to	
  you	
  over	
  the	
  coming	
  year	
  as	
  we	
  go	
  through	
  the	
  12	
  months	
  of	
  teleseminar	
  coaching	
  calls.
BUT,	
  I	
  can	
  give	
  you	
  the	
  tools,	
  the	
  education,	
  the	
  live	
  coaching...	
  ...and	
  it’s	
  ABSOLUTELY	
  USELESS	
  if	
  you	
  do	
  
nothing	
  with	
  it!	
  YOU	
  have	
  to	
  implement	
  it.	
  Do	
  one	
  thing	
  at	
  a	
  time.
Leverage	
  the	
  calendar	
  and	
  plan	
  it	
  out.	
  Hire	
  help	
  if	
  you	
  need.	
  JUST	
  GET	
  IT	
  OUT	
  THE	
  DOOR.	
  Your	
  cash	
  flow	
  will	
  
quickly	
  grow.
Your	
  client	
  relationships	
  will	
  improve.	
  And	
  your	
  business	
  will	
  thrive.	
  But	
  ONLY	
  if	
  you	
  take	
  action...	
  MASSIVE	
  
ACTION.
I’m	
  here	
  to	
  help...	
  but	
  you	
  need	
  to	
  get	
  your	
  ego	
  and	
  opinions	
  out	
  of	
  the	
  way	
  until	
  you’ve	
  TESTED	
  this	
  
approach.
It	
  works.
I	
  have
